\DoxyCodeLine{671 \textcolor{comment}{// ImDrawList: Helper function to calculate a circle's segment count given its radius and a "{}maximum error"{} value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{672 \textcolor{comment}{// Estimation of number of circle segment based on error is derived using method described in https://stackoverflow.com/a/2244088/15194693}}
\DoxyCodeLine{673 \textcolor{comment}{// Number of segments (N) is calculated using equation:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{674 \textcolor{comment}{//   N = ceil ( pi / acos(1 -\/ error / r) )     where r > 0, error <= r}}
\DoxyCodeLine{675 \textcolor{comment}{// Our equation is significantly simpler that one in the post thanks for choosing segment that is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{676 \textcolor{comment}{// perpendicular to X axis. Follow steps in the article from this starting condition and you will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{677 \textcolor{comment}{// will get this result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{678 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{679 \textcolor{comment}{// Rendering circles with an odd number of segments, while mathematically correct will produce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{680 \textcolor{comment}{// asymmetrical results on the raster grid. Therefore we're rounding N to next even number (7-\/>8, 8-\/>8, 9-\/>10 etc.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{681 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{682 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_ROUNDUP\_TO\_EVEN(\_V)                                  ((((\_V) + 1) / 2) * 2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{683 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MIN                     4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{684 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MAX                     512}}
\DoxyCodeLine{685 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC(\_RAD,\_MAXERROR)    ImClamp(IM\_ROUNDUP\_TO\_EVEN((int)ImCeil(IM\_PI / ImAcos(1 -\/ ImMin((\_MAXERROR), (\_RAD)) / (\_RAD)))), IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MIN, IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MAX)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{686 }
\DoxyCodeLine{687 \textcolor{comment}{// Raw equation from IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC rewritten for 'r' and 'error'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{688 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC\_R(\_N,\_MAXERROR)    ((\_MAXERROR) / (1 -\/ ImCos(IM\_PI / ImMax((float)(\_N), IM\_PI))))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{689 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC\_ERROR(\_N,\_RAD)     ((1 -\/ ImCos(IM\_PI / ImMax((float)(\_N), IM\_PI))) / (\_RAD))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{690 }
\DoxyCodeLine{691 \textcolor{comment}{// ImDrawList: Lookup table size for adaptive arc drawing, cover full circle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{692 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef IM\_DRAWLIST\_ARCFAST\_TABLE\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{693 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_ARCFAST\_TABLE\_SIZE                          48 }\textcolor{comment}{// Number of samples in lookup table.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{694 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{695 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_ARCFAST\_SAMPLE\_MAX                          IM\_DRAWLIST\_ARCFAST\_TABLE\_SIZE }\textcolor{comment}{// Sample index \_PathArcToFastEx() for 360 angle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{696 }
